–ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É —è —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—é relocate_item_my, –µ—ë –∫–ª–∞–¥–µ–º –≤ –ª—é–±–æ–π –≤–∞—à —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç.
function relocate_item_my(victim, section, type)
  if db.actor and victim then
    if type == "in" then

      if victim:object(section) ~= nil then
        victim:transfer_item(victim:object(section), db.actor)
      end
    elseif type == "out" then
      db.actor:transfer_item(db.actor:object(section), victim)
    end
    news_manager.relocate_item(db.actor, type, section)
  end
end

end

C:\SDK_no_storyline\gamedata\scripts\ui_main_menu.script

function main_menu:OnKeyboard(dik, keyboard_action)  --virtual function
  CUIScriptWnd.OnKeyboard(self,dik,keyboard_action)
  local bind = dik_to_bind(dik)
  local console = get_console()
  
  if keyboard_action == ui_events.WINDOW_KEY_PRESSED then
    if dik == DIK_keys.DIK_ESCAPE then
      if level.present() and (db.actor ~= nil) and db.actor:alive() then
        console:execute("main_menu off")
      end
    end
    
    if dik == DIK_keys.DIK_SPACE then
      self:StartGame()
    end

    if dik == DIK_keys.DIK_F1 then
      local gv = db.actor:game_vertex_id()
      local lv = db.actor:level_vertex_id()
      local pos = db.actor:position()
      local posx = pos.x
      local posy = pos.y
      local posz = pos.z
      local dir = db.actor:direction()
      local dirx = dir.x
      local diry = dir.y
      local dirz = dir.z
      news_manager.send_tip(db.actor, "Position:".."\\n".."X: "..posx.."\\n".."Y: "..posy.."\\n".."Z: "..posz.."\\n".."Direction: ".."\\n".."X: "..dirx.."\\n".."Y: "..diry.."\\n".."Z: "..dirz.."\\n".."Game Vertex ID: "..gv.."\\n".."Level Vertex ID: "..lv.."\\n".."That's all.", nil, nil, 100000)
      console:execute("main_menu off")
    end
    
    -- if dik == DIK_keys.DIK_W then
      -- console:execute("main_menu off")
      -- fast_travel.create_level_changer(vector():set(162.613, -0.001, 65.842),42218,1179)
    -- end
    
    if dik == DIK_keys.DIK_Q then
      self:OnMessageQuitWin()
    end
  
  end
   
  return true
end

function fix_val_watchtower()
    local sobj = alife():object("val_watchtower4_bandit_guard")
    if sobj then
      local pk = get_netpk( sobj, 1 )
      ASSERT( ( pk and pk:isOk() ), "can't read netpacket of %s", sobj:name() )
      local data = pk:get()
      data.object_flags = bit_or( data.object_flags, object_flags.SwitchOnline ) -- —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ñ–ª–∞–≥ SwitchOnline
      --data.object_flags = bit_and( data.object_flags, bit_not( object_flags.OfflineNoMove ) ) -- —Å–Ω—è—Ç—å —Ñ–ª–∞–≥ OfflineNoMove
      pk:set( data )
    log3( "--[%s]: Fixed object_flags for [%s]!", script_name(), sobj:name() )
    end
end

–°–ø–∞–≤–Ω –≤–µ—Ä—Ç–æ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞–¥ —Å–æ–±–æ–π, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—à–Ω –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ–º –∫–∞–∫–æ–π –Ω–∞–¥–æ.

local position = db.actor:position()
position.y = position.y + 50
sak.spawn_military_tech_pack(alife():create("helicopter",position, db.actor:level_vertex_id(), db.actor:game_vertex_id()) ,"helicopter", "scripts\\esc\\esc_blockpost_btr.ltx")


–§—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è —Å–ø–∞–≤–Ω–∞, –µ—ë –∫–ª–∞–¥–µ–º –∫—É–¥–∞ –≤–∞–º —É–¥–æ–±–Ω–æ.
function spawn_military_tech_pack(obj, spawn_item, spawn_item_logic)
    local pk = get_netpk(obj, 1)
    ASSERT((pk and pk:isOk()), "can't read netpacket of %s", obj:name())
    local data = pk:get()
    data.custom_data:setString("[logic]\ncfg = " .. spawn_item_logic)
    if spawn_item == "helicopter" then
        data.engine_sound = "alexmx\\helicopter"
    elseif spawn_item == "m_car" then
        data.health = 1
    end
    pk:set(data)
    return obj
end
